## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of time t and current population P. This is a classic population dynamics problem where growth rate depends on population size through various density-dependent and density-independent mechanisms.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- {'name': 'Exponential (Malthusian) growth', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P', 'scenario': 'Density-independent growth with unlimited resources'}
- {'name': 'Logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P)', 'scenario': 'Density-dependent growth with carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Gompertz growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate decreasing logarithmically as population increases'}
- {'name': 'Theta-logistic growth', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2)', 'scenario': 'Generalized logistic with nonlinear density dependence'}
- {'name': 'Allee effect (strong)', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate negative below a critical population threshold'}
- {'name': 'Weak Allee effect', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (c2 + P)', 'scenario': 'Reduced per-capita growth at low density without negative growth'}
- {'name': 'Richards growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) / c2', 'scenario': 'Asymmetric sigmoidal growth generalization'}
- {'name': 'Power-law growth', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1', 'scenario': 'Fractal or allometric scaling of growth rate with population'}
- {'name': 'Von Bertalanffy-type growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Balance between anabolic (power-law) and catabolic (linear) processes'}
- {'name': 'Time-dependent Malthusian growth', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t)', 'scenario': 'Exponential growth with time-varying growth rate'}
- {'name': 'Harvesting/mortality logistic', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Logistic growth with constant per-capita harvesting'}
- {'name': 'Oscillatory growth modulation', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t))', 'scenario': 'Logistic growth with seasonal or periodic environmental forcing'}
- {'name': 'Quadratic density dependence', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3', 'scenario': 'Polynomial expansion of density-dependent effects'}

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent regulation → multiplicative factor (1 - c*P) or (1 - (c*P)**n) limiting growth at high P
- Allee effects → additional multiplicative factor (P - c) introducing a minimum viable population threshold
- Per-capita growth rate analysis → dP_dt/P should simplify to reveal the functional form of density dependence
- Carrying capacity structure → growth rate equals zero at P = 1/c, look for roots of dP_dt in P
- Seasonal/periodic forcing → sinusoidal modulation sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) multiplied by growth terms
- Competing growth and decay processes → difference of power laws c0*P**a - c1*P**b with b > a
- Logarithmic density dependence → log(c/P) terms indicate Gompertz-type deceleration, slower than logistic
- Time-explicit dependence → if dP_dt depends on t directly, suggests non-autonomous dynamics or environmental change

## GT Analysis

The GT numerical expression is:
```
0.1699888096710614*(-1 + P/1.0472843670254641)*(1 - P/10.210545156320043)*P + 0.1699888096710614*(1 - P/10.210545156320043)*P + 0.1699888096710614*(1 - exp(-0.09709294493863778*P))*P
```

Let me simplify. Let me denote α = 0.16999, β = 1/1.04728 ≈ 0.95486, γ = 1/10.2105 ≈ 0.09794, δ = 0.09709.

Expanding term by term:

**Term 1:** α*(-1 + βP)*(1 - γP)*P = α*(βP - 1)*(1 - γP)*P
= α*P*(βP - 1 - βγP² + γP)
= α*(βP² - P - βγP³ + γP²)
= α*(-βγP³ + (β+γ)P² - P)

**Term 2:** α*(1 - γP)*P = α*(P - γP²)

**Term 3:** α*(1 - exp(-δP))*P = α*(P - P·exp(-δP))

Combining Terms 1+2+3:
- P³ term: -αβγ P³
- P² term: α(β+γ)P² - αγP²  = αβP²
- P term: -αP + αP = 0
- Exponential term: -α·P·exp(-δP) + αP

Wait, let me redo:
Term 1: α*(-βγP³ + (β+γ)P² - P)
Term 2: α*(P - γP²)
Term 3: α*(P - P·exp(-δP))

Sum:
- P³: -αβγ
- P²: α(β+γ) - αγ = αβ
- P: -α + α + α = α
- exp: -α·P·exp(-δP)

So GT = **-αβγ·P³ + αβ·P² + α·P - α·P·exp(-δP)**

= P*(-αβγ·P² + αβ·P + α - α·exp(-δP))

= **α·P·(-βγP² + βP + 1 - exp(-δP))**

Or equivalently: GT = c₃P³ + c₂P² + c₁P + c_exp·P·exp(c_e·P)

where:
- c₃ = -αβγ (negative)
- c₂ = αβ (positive)  
- c₁ = α
- c_exp = -α
- c_e = -δ

So GT has the form: **a·P³ + b·P² + c·P + d·P·exp(e·P)**

Now let me check each candidate against this structural form: polynomial P³ + P² + P + P·exp(kP).

Note: there's no constant term (when P=0, GT=0).

### Checking candidates for the form: a·P³ + b·P² + c·P + d·P·exp(e·P)

**Candidate 5:** P*(P³c0 + P²c1 + Pc2 + c3*(P+1)*exp(Pc4) + c5)/(P+1)

Expanding: P*(P³c0 + P²c1 + Pc2 + c3·P·exp(Pc4) + c3·exp(Pc4) + c5)/(P+1)

This has both P·exp and exp terms in numerator divided by (P+1). Can we make this work?

If we do polynomial long division of (P³c0 + ...)/(P+1), this gets complicated. The exp terms would need to cancel the (P+1) denominator, which requires specific structure. Let me check: we need c3*(P+1)*exp(Pc4)/(P+1) = c3*exp(Pc4). Then remaining: P*(P³c0 + P²c1 + Pc2 + c5)/(P+1).

For P*(P³c0 + P²c1 + Pc2 + c5)/(P+1) to be a polynomial, (P+1) must divide (P³c0 + P²c1 + Pc2 + c5). Setting P=-1: -c0 + c1 - c2 + c5 = 0, i.e., c5 = c0 - c1 + c2.

Then P³c0 + P²c1 + Pc2 + c5 = (P+1)*(c0P² + (c1-c0)P + (c2-c1+c0)).

Result: P*(c0P² + (c1-c0)P + (c2-c1+c0)) + c3·P·exp(Pc4)

= c0·P³ + (c1-c0)·P² + (c2-c1+c0)·P + c3·P·exp(Pc4)

This is exactly **aP³ + bP² + cP + dP·exp(eP)**! ✓
